<p>Uncertain, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draf.html>draf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dregs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*drabaz</i>). <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">drabbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">silt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***dragen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dragen.html>dragen</a> (926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">drāgen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:dragan.html>dragan</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*draganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:draw.html>draw</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pull.html>pull</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:carry.html>carry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dragonder.html>dragonder</a> (76299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Dragoner</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> pejorative <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> might <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reference.html>reference</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>Aal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dragonder.html>Dragonder</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woman.html>woman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> lived <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> seventeenth <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eighteenth.html>eighteenth</a> centuries <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> dressed <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> dragoon, <a href = vnd.unilang:though.html>though</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:only.html>only</a> originated <a href = vnd.unilang:well.html>well</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:her.html>her</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:death.html>death</a>. Otherwise <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:could.html>could</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:similar.html>similar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:development.html>development</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> “large <a href = vnd.unilang:ugly.html>ugly</a> woman” <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draak.html>draak</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreunen.html>dreunen</a> (61237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:dronen.html>dronen</a></i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:dronen.html>dronen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">drynja</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language"><a href = vnd.unilang:gothic.html>Gothic</a></a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌳𐍂𐌿𐌽𐌾𐌿𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drunjus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:long.html>long</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vowel.html>vowel</a> <span class="IPA">/øː/</span> precludes <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derivation.html>derivation</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hypothetical.html>hypothetical</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*drunjaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drietal.html>drietal</a> (40879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
